< Review>
First time checking out this place, and I must say it was a pretty terrible experience. Staff were pretty hospitable at first, but once we ordered and got everything, service pretty much went down hill from there. We had an issue with our hookah. After informing the staff several times there was an issue, they didn't really do much to resolve it. All of us ordered tea, which practically tasted like plain water.

All in all the hookah was pretty terrible, service wasn't all that great, and don't order tea there if you're a genuine tea lover. Definitely don't recommend this place at all.< /Review>

< Text>
This place is so low key, you can't tell it's a hookah lounge from the outside. Inside it's pretty chill and low key as well, dim-lit, good vibes. They play really good music, and the hookahs are really good too. Service is nice. They only have drinks, no food. You can order for delivery from a nearby Mediterranean place but you can't eat on there after 9 or 10. I feel like a lot of the people who come here are regulars of some degree. Overall, it's a good experience.< /Text>

< review>
New in 2020, this dog play area is expansive and generally pretty busy. It's also in a gorgeous setting in the park right near the bison paddock. It's a great jumping off or ending point for a walk in the park, as there is a decent amount of parking available.

It features a sizable area for small dogs as well as a larger area for big dogs. Both areas have a section of artificial turf and a section with sand and eucalyptus logs, with concrete walkways in between. There are park benches for pet owners to watch their pups play and dog+human water fountains.<//review>

Newly renovated with ample of parking.

I brought my 12 lbs dog here and I feel safe for him to play in the area. Big enough for small and big dogs to run around.

Both areas have secure fencing, double gate entrances (that's a convenience) and provide varied surfaces of cement, artificial turf and sand. The large parking lot was full when I arrived so I parked along the park road. There are plenty of trails around the fenced areas for walking/strolling and the view of the adjacent Buffalo enclosure adds a nice touch. No human bathrooms, but nearby attractions do have restroom facilities.</review>< Rating>

<Rating>5<//Rating><text>There's a small dog section and an all dog section. Both sections have an artificial turf area and area that is all sand with se obstacles to play around on. There are a couple of  double-gate entrances to each section, plus there are a couple of gates that can be passed through that connect the small and all dog section.

Overall it's well maintained and nice. The small dog section is pretty large, and the all dog section is huge. It can get extremely busy, but there is usually enough room to safely social distance. Plus, since there are multiple entrances it cuts down on congestion and having the gates being opened constantly. Definitely coming back.< /text></record>

< text>
Great dog park with a variety of dogs and responsible owners. One told me on weekdays there are a lot of dog walkers resulting in crowded and possibly unfriendly environment, usually starting from 9am to afternoon, it dies down a bit after 4 or 5. The rest of time it is occupied mostly by dog owners, early mornings and evenings on weekdays or the entire weekends.

Parking was a bit hard to find. If you are on Fulton, come through 36th Street and go pass the senior center all the way till the end.<//text>

<Text>It is a good place to take your fur baby to burn off energy. But alot of dogs can be there during the workday and maybe busy on the weekends. The surface is sand so watch out for puddles and mud during the rainy season. There are 2 water stations with faucets for both dogs and humans located inside and outside the fenced-in area. It is on the north side of the Bison paddock so you might get lucky and see a Bison or two. The park lot there is small, it holds about 15 cars. There are benches and tables there for us humans or tired pups to relax on. There are plans to separate this into two areas, One for small dogs and one for large dogs.< /Text>< Pictures>

<userid>102988175266814838983< /userid>< Text>
Stay away! Especially if you don't know your rights as a tenant and the legal protocal landlords are supposed to follow which this place does not. Wendy (financial administrator) thinks she owns the place and acts like it.

The maintenance staff was nice despite 3 seperate attempts to fix our front door that had a huge gap where weather stripping was supposed to be. Several fellow tenants were especially helpful and friendly, giving us advice for our situation and even assisting with getting our fridge up 2 flights of awkward stairs when we first moved in. Our original rent was roughly 995 month. 6 months later and prices in Victorville, Hesperia and Apple Valley have shot up tremendously... Our apartment is now being charged 1100 a month. This place is a revolving door of tenants and our rental was surrounded by empty ones after only being there 2 months.

The financial administrator refused to work with us when we were late on a month's rent even though we'd presented all of it along with the offer to pay any other late fees in installments. It's actually illegal for the administrator to do this and the office is supposed to provide detailed information about the actual owners of the complex because they are the ones tenants need to meet with to discuss payments. Everyone I've spoken to has said that it's extremely fishy that the owner's contact information isn't provided and that they have no right to charge for so many different things and not allow any negotiating. The financial administrator will be more than happy to tell you to pay up or get out in the middle of your court case as well so don't even bother trying to fight it, just stall so you get more time to move out. And if you happen to forget something in your rush to move out, you'll have to fork over another $700 just to get back in to retrieve it.

There's also been drug activity, assaults, thefts and a child kidnapping just within the past year here. So if the above wasn't convincing enough, maybe this tidbit will do it.

Edit: Aaaaand to add insult to injury, they will withold your proof of residency which other potential landlords need before they can approve you to get into a new residence after escaping this place. Thanks for the extra slap in the face Mountain Vista!
